1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers</span></div></td></tr></table></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On November 17, 2025, Celeste Burgoyne notified us of her resignation as President, Americas and Global Guest Innovation. Ms. Burgoyne will remain active in the business through the end of the calendar year and her employment will terminate effective December 31, 2025. </span></div><div style="text-indent:24.75pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:23.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On November 21, 2025, we announced that our board of directors has appointed Andre Maestrini as lululemon&#8217;s president and chief commercial officer, effective immediately. Mr. Maestrini has served as executive vice president, international, since January 2021, overseeing our international expansion across APAC, EMEA and China Mainland. He has been responsible for leading our global offices and driving brand growth across multiple international markets and channels. Before joining lululemon, Mr. Maestrini spent 14 years at adidas in various senior roles, including global general manager of sport business units and managing director of Latin America. Earlier in his career, he held marketing positions at The Coca-Cola Company, Danone, and Kraft Jacobs Suchard. Mr. Maestrini holds a master&#8217;s degree in Marketing from ESSEC Business School in Paris, France.</span></div><div style="text-indent:23.75pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:23.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In connection with Mr. Maestrini&#8217;s appointment as president and chief commercial officer, we entered into an employment agreement with Mr. Maestrini providing for a base salary of USD $950,000, eligibility for an annual bonus if specified performance goals are met, participation in our benefit plans, and customary severance protections. This description does not purport to be complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the employment agreement, a copy of which is attached as Exhibit 10.1.</span></div><div The rate of pay due in respect of each public holiday or day's paid holiday will be calculated on the basis of 1&#47;260th of your Salary.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You must give at least 2 weeks&#8217; notice of proposed holiday days. Holidays are to be taken at such time or times as may be approved in advance by the Board. Employees are expected to be available from the 15th December until the 15th January. This is the busiest trading time for our ecommerce business and stores and as such is considered a vacation blackout period.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Company and you agree that in any holiday year you will be deemed to take any holiday accruing under the Working Time Regulations 1998 first.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.5&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Any leave not taken by the end of the holiday year in which it accrued will be lost, unless the Board has otherwise agreed in advance, or you are permitted to carry over any leave under the Working Time Regulations 1998. There is no payment in lieu of any holiday untaken at the end of the holiday year, except on termination (see below).</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.6&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Where, as a result of taking a period of sick leave, you have been unable to take some or all of your holiday during the relevant holiday year, you will be entitled to carry over any holiday accruing under Regulation 13 of the Working Time Regulations 1998 to the extent it has not already been taken in the relevant holiday year. Any carried over holiday will be lost if it is not taken within 18 months of the end of the holiday year in which it accrued.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.7&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;We reserve the right to require you to take (or not to take) all or part of any outstanding holiday during your notice period. Any accrued but unused holiday entitlement shall be deemed to be taken during any period of garden leave under clause 26.1.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.8&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;On termination of your employment, your entitlement to accrued holiday pay will be directly in proportion to your service during the holiday year in which the termination takes place. If on termination you have taken holiday in excess of your entitlement, we will be entitled to deduct from any sums payable to you a sum in respect of each day's holiday taken in excess of your entitlement.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">17.9&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;If your employment is terminated under clause 27.1, you will not be entitled to any payment in respect of holiday which would have otherwise accrued during the remainder of the notice period.</font></div><div style="height:113.04pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;text-align:right"><font self-certification forms which are required by the Company and&#47;or lululemon athletica UK Ltd. If the incapacity continues for a period of eight days or more, you will provide a medical certificate to cover the duration of such absence. You must produce medical certificates to cover any further period of absence. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">18.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;If you are unable to attend work because of illness or injury then subject to clause 25.1(h) and provided you have complied with the requirements of this clause 18, you will be entitled to receive Statutory Sick Pay (SSP) during such periods of absence if you satisfy the relevant statutory requirements. The lululemon Group operates an income protection scheme for employees with long-term absence due to sickness which you may be entitled to benefit from.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">18.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;For the avoidance of doubt, the provisions of this clause 18 will not prejudice or limit in any way our right to terminate this agreement pursuant to clause 4 and clause 25 or otherwise pursuant to its terms.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">18.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;In order for the Company to exercise its rights and comply with its employment law obligations, you shall, at the request of the Company, agree to have a medical examination performed by a doctor (or other medical adviser, including the Company's occupational health advisers) appointed and paid for by the lululemon Group. instrument or act falls within the authority conferred by this clause&#59; such a certificate will be deemed to be conclusive evidence that this is the case.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">21.9&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You accept that no future agreement between you and the Company or any lululemon Group Company, dealing with the ownership or licensing of any Intellectual Property Rights in any Inventions and&#47;or Works, shall be enforceable unless and until it is in writing signed on behalf of a lululemon Group Company by a director (not being you).</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font yourself or through any other person or entity do anything that would require a licence of any of the Company's or the lululemon Group&#8217;s Intellectual Property Rights (including, without limitation, those assigned by you to under this agreement or by operation of law) without first obtaining the Company's prior written consent (which may be given, withheld and&#47;or conditioned by the Company at its sole discretion).</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">21.11&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You agree that you will not use or commercially exploit any of the Company's or the lululemon Group&#8217;s Intellectual Property Rights (including, without limitation, those assigned by you to the Company under this agreement or by operation of law) after the termination of your employment, without the Company's prior written consent (which may be given, withheld and&#47;or conditioned by the Company at its sole discretion).</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font clauses 20, 21.10 and 21.11 above, you shall keep details of any Inventions (including, without limitation, the existence of any Inventions) and&#47;or Works in relation to which Intellectual Property Rights may subsist confidential. You shall not, without the Company's consent, apply for patent, registered design or other registered protection in respect of any invention or design or other Intellectual Property Rights capable of registration, the rights in which belong to the Company (or its nominee). You shall promptly inform the Company if you apply for patent or registered design or other registered protection in respect of any invention or design made by you or other Intellectual Property Rights capable of registration, the rights in which belong to you.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">21.13&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Without prejudice to the other provisions of this agreement, the Company owns all documents, files, data and prototypes or models that you create during the course of your employment (and&#47;or as a result of any duties specifically assigned to you by the Company from time to time) or by using materials, tools, information or opportunities made available through your employment. You must keep these secure and held in accordance with the requirements of this agreement and must promptly deliver up to the Company all such materials at our request and in any event on termination of this agreement for any reason.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">21.14&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The provisions of this clause 21 shall remain in full force and effect following the termination of this agreement for any reason, whether such termination is lawful or not.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">22&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;RESTRICTIVE COVENANTS</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">22.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;In this clause 22, the following words have the following meanings&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:69.85pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#34;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">Business</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">&#34; means the business of the design, manufacture, sale and distribution of yoga and other sports and leisure based clothing and apparel and any other </font></div><div style="height:113.04pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;15</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:56.88pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:13pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:69.85pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">business carried on by the Company and any lululemon Group Company from time to time&#59;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:69.85pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#34;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">Company Intellectual Property</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">&#34; shall mean the Business or any part of the Business which in either case&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:105pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;is carried on by the Company or any lululemon Group Company at the date of termination of your employment&#59; or</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:105pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(ii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;was carried on by the Company or by any lululemon Group Company at any time during the period of six (6) months immediately prior either to the start of a period of Garden Leave or to the date of termination of your employment where there is no period of Garden Leave&#59; shall mean any senior employee of the Company or any lululemon Group Company employed at the date of termination of your employment in the capacity of director or in any research, technical, IT, financial, marketing or sales function or other managerial role whom you have managed or with whom you have worked at any time during the period of twelve (12) months immediately prior to the termination of your employment, and shall not include any employee employed in an administrative, clerical, manual or secretarial capacity&#59;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:69.85pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#34;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">Restricted Supplier</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">&#34; shall mean&#58; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:105pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the United Kingdom (being England, Scotland, Wales and Northern Ireland)&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:105pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(iii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;any other country in which the Company or any other lululemon Group Company&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:139.9pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(A)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;carried on any Restricted Business or provided any goods or services in connection with any Restricted Business at the date of termination of your employment&#59; and&#47;or</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:139.9pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(B)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;had management responsibility for&#59; and&#47;or</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:139.9pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(C)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;obtained confidential information in respect of.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">22.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You acknowledge that following termination of your employment, you will be in a position to compete unfairly with the Company as a result of the confidential information, trade secrets and knowledge about the business, operations, customers, employees and trade connections of the Company and the lululemon Group you have acquired or will acquire and through the connections that you have developed and will develop during your employment.  You therefore agree to enter into the restrictions in this paragraph for the purpose of protecting the Company's legitimate business interests and in particular the confidential information, goodwill and the stable trained workforce of the Company and the lululemon Group.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font that you shall not without the prior written consent of the Company (such consent not to be unreasonably withheld), directly or indirectly, on your own behalf, or on behalf of any person, firm or company in connection with any business which is or is intended or about to be competitive with the Restricted Business (as defined above) or in relation to the provision of any goods or services employment, solicit or entice away, or attempt to entice away from the Company or any lululemon Group Company any Restricted Employee (as defined above)&#59;</font></div><div press releases, articles, letters, telephone calls, telephone messages, e-mail messages, or in postings on the Internet on websites, or to newsgroups or to listservers.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">33.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The lululemon Group&#8217;s disciplinary and grievance procedures applicable to you are set out in the lululemon athletica UK Ltd. staff handbook. These procedures do not form part of your contract of employment.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">33.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;If you have any grievance relating to your employment, you should raise it in the first instance with Susan Gelinas, Chief People &#38; Culture Officer, in accordance with the Company's grievance procedure.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">33.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;If you are dissatisfied with any disciplinary decision taken against you, you may appeal to Calvin McDonald, CEO.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">34&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;DATA PROTECTION</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">34.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Company places the highest importance on compliance with all applicable Data Protection Laws.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">34.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Company shall hold and process personal data (including special categories of personal data) relating to you in manual and automated filing systems. Details about how and why the Company generally processes employee personal data (including your personal data) are set out in the Company's staff privacy notice, the current version of which is available on the intranet and from HR. By entering into this agreement, you confirm that you have read and understood the Company's staff privacy notice.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">34.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;It is important that all Company employees take appropriate steps to protect personal data and use it lawfully. Accordingly, you must treat all personal data relating to any person, whether within or outside the Company, which you acquire in the proper course of your employment in effect as if it were confidential information of the Company and shall not do&#47;or omit to do anything that would put the Company in breach of Data Protection Laws. You also confirm that you will comply with the Company's current data protection policy and other Company policies relating to the security and use of personal data, copies of which are available on the intranet and from HR. A failure to comply with these policies may be dealt with under the Company's disciplinary procedure and, in deliberate or very serious cases of data misuse, may be treated as gross misconduct potentially leading to summary dismissal.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">34.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You agree to keep the Company informed of any changes to your personal data.</font></div><div style="height:113.04pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;24</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:56.88pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:13pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">35&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;BRIBERY AND CORRUPTION</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">35.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Company expects the highest standards of integrity in relation to employees' dealings with lululemon&#8217;s customers, suppliers, agents and subcontractors and with any government official.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">35.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;For the purposes of this clause&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:69.85pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;A bribe is any gift, loan, fee, reward or other advantage given to or received from any person in order to obtain, retain or direct business or to secure any other improper advantage in the conduct of business and includes a kickback on any portion of a contract payment&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:69.85pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Hospitality, entertainment and gifts includes but is not limited to the offer or receipt of gifts, meals, goods, services, favours, loans, trips, accommodation and the use of property or invitations to events, functions or other social gatherings.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">35.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You are prohibited from offering, giving, authorising or accepting a bribe in any form. You are also prohibited from using any other route or channel to provide a bribe to or receive a bribe from any of the lululemon Group&#8217;s customers, suppliers, agents or subcontractors or any government official.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">35.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;You are not permitted to give or receive hospitality, entertainment or gifts to or from any customer, supplier, agent, subcontractor, any government official or any other person without the express written authority of the lululemon Group. If you are given or offered hospitality, entertainment or gifts (regardless of value) by any customer, supplier, agent, subcontractor, any government official or any other person with whom the lululemon Group deals or has business contacts, you must advise the Board immediately. The Board will then advise on the action to be taken in the circumstances to ensure that both the lululemon Group&#8217;s and your interests are protected.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">35.5&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Where you suspect, believe or know that an act of bribery or corruption is being considered or carried out, you are required to report this to the Board.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">36&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;COLLECTIVE AGREEMENTS</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">There are no collective agreements with trade unions that directly affect the terms and conditions of your employment.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:122%">37&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;NOTICES</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:122%">37.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Any notice to be given to you under this agreement may be given to you personally or sent to you by pre-paid first class letter addressed to you at your last known place of residence. Any notice to be given to the Company should be addressed to the Legal Department and may be served by leaving it at or sending it by pre-paid first class letter to Erin Nicholas, SVP, Senior Deputy General Counsel &#38; Corporate Secretary, at the Company's registered office for the time being.  Notice may also be provided at any other address, individual or electronic communication number, as may be designated by notice given by either party to the other.  </font></div><div style="height:113.04pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;text-align:right"><font personally, at the time the notice is left at the address or given to the addressee&#59; or in the case of pre-paid first class post, at 9am on the second business day after posting, or in the case of email at the time of transmission.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font accordance with the terms and conditions of this agreement.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font shall be deemed to have been terminated by mutual consent with effect from the Commencement Date.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:13pt;padding-left:35pt;text-indent:-35pt"><font (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) today announced that Celeste Burgoyne, President of the Americas and Global Guest Innovation, has decided to leave the company for a new opportunity outside of the industry. She will remain with lululemon until the end of December 2025 to ensure a smooth transition.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Ms. Burgoyne joined lululemon in 2006 and became the company&#8217;s first President in 2020. Throughout her tenure, she has assumed roles of increasing responsibility and led the North America business through periods of rapid growth and expansion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;We are grateful for Celeste&#8217;s leadership and significant contributions to lululemon&#8217;s business and culture over the past 19 years. She has been instrumental in growing our footprint in the Americas, creating high-quality guest experiences, and mentoring our teams across the organization,&#8221; said Calvin McDonald, Chief Executive Officer, lululemon. &#8220;I deeply appreciate her partnership and friendship, and we wish her all the best in the future.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;My time at lululemon has been both inspiring and rewarding beyond belief,&#8221; said Ms. Burgoyne. &#8220;I am so proud of what we have accomplished as an organization since I joined in 2006 and know the team will take the company to even greater heights in the years to come. I look forward to continuing to support the brand as a lifelong fan.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In conjunction with this announcement, lululemon has made the decision to consolidate regional leadership across the company and appoint Andr&#233; Maestrini as President and Chief Commercial Officer, effective immediately. Mr. Maestrini will continue to report directly to Mr. McDonald.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In this newly created role, Mr. Maestrini will provide integrated oversight of all of lululemon&#8217;s regions, stores, and digital channels globally. He will also oversee lululemon&#8217;s global commercial strategy with a focus on continued market expansion, revenue generation, and accelerating best practice sharing, across all regions including North America.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Mr. Maestrini joined lululemon in 2021 as Executive Vice President of International. In his current role, he has overseen lululemon&#8217;s operations in EMEA, APAC, and China Mainland, and has helped to more than quadruple lululemon&#8217;s international revenues.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Andr&#233; has demonstrated a proven ability to unlock opportunities, advance our global expansion, and deliver growth across multiple markets,&#8221; said Mr. McDonald. &#8220;Leveraging operational discipline, deep guest insights, and extensive brand-building experience, Andr&#233; is the ideal person to lead our business across all markets, including North America, as we remain focused on delivering value for our guests, employees, and shareholders.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Before joining lululemon, Mr. Maestrini spent 14 years at adidas in various senior roles across the globe. During this time, he served in a number of General Manager positions where he helped grow the company&#8217;s global sports categories and regional markets. Prior to adidas, Mr. Maestrini held marketing roles at The Coca-Cola Company, Danone, and Kraft Jacobs Suchard.</font></div><div id="i3b63d41244c341e7bcfbf2833430db85_4"></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About lululemon </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">lululemon (NASDAQ&#58;LULU) is a technical athletic apparel, footwear, and accessories company for yoga, running, training, and most other activities, creating transformational products and experiences that build meaningful connections, unlocking greater possibility and wellbeing for all. Setting the bar in innovation of fabrics and functional designs, lululemon works with yogis and athletes in local communities around the world for continuous research and product feedback.
